60b3(mdo sde): yon tan dbang phyung de la smad ma mchis// rgyal po chen po dge sbyong go'u ta ma de ni stobs bcu dang ldan pa'o// smras pa/ bram ze chen po de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu po de dag gang / smras pa/
60b4(mdo sde): rgyal po chen po 'di lta ste/ 'di na de bzhin gshegs pa ni gnas la yang gnas su yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu mkhyen/ gnas ma lags pa la yang gnas par yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu/
60b5(mdo sde): mkhyen te/ rgyal po chen po 'di ni dge sbyong go'u ta ma de'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs dang po'o// de bzhin gshegs pa de ni 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i las yang dag
60b6(mdo sde): par blangs pa rnams gnas dang / rigs dang / rnam par smin pa las yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu mkhyen to// 'jig rten gyi khams du ma dang / khams sna tshogs pa rnams yang dag pa'i/
60b7(mdo sde): lta ba bzhin du rab tu mkhyen to// sems can gzhan dag dang / gang zag gzhan rnams kyi mos pa du ma dang / mos pa sna tshogs yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu mkhyen to// sems can gzhan
61a1(mdo sde): dag dang / gang zag gzhan rnams kyi dbang po mchog dang / mchog ma yin pa mkhyen pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu mkhyen to// thams cad 'gro ba'i lam yang
61a2(mdo sde): dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu mkhyen to// sems can gzhan dag dang / gang zag gzhan rnams kyi dbang po dang / stobs dang / byang chub kyi yan lag dang / bsam gtan dang ka rnam par
61a3(mdo sde): thar pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / snyoms par 'jug pa rnams kyi kun nas nyon mongs pa dang / rnam par byang ba dang ldan pa dang / rnam par dag pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu mkhyen to// /
61a4(mdo sde): sngon gyi gnas rnam pa du ma rjes su dran te/ tshe rabs gcig kyang rjes su dran zhing / tshe rabs bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag du ma'i bar dag kyang rnam pa dang bcas pa dang / sa phyogs dang bcus pa/
61a5(mdo sde): dang rgya mtshan dang bcas par sngon gyi gnas rnam pa du ma rjes su dran no// de lnga'i spyan rnam par dag pa mi'i las 'das pas/ sems can 'chi 'pho dang / skye bo las bde 'gro nga
61a6(mdo sde): ngan 'gror skye ba rnams gzigs so// zag pa zad pas/ dag pa med pa/ sems rnam par grol ba dang / shes rab rnam par grol ba yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu mkhyen /
61a7(mdo sde): di de hU~M ma badzin ga gags pa'i thabs bcu 'o// rgyal bcan po'i shin bzhin gshegs pa'i rtsibs bcu 'angs/ stobs de dag nga rjen pas
61b1(mdo sde): gshegs pa'i stobs bcu mang 'a zhes bgyis// de'i slad du de sngon ma mchis lags so// del 'di gad ces kyi ste/ gnas dang de bzhin gnas ma lags// yang dag de bzhin na
61b2(mdo sde): mkhyen te// dpa' bo chen po yang dag gsung // de la skyon ni mchis so// de ni 'das pa'i dus la yang // ma chags pa yi ye shes 'jug/ da ltar byung dang ma 'ongs la// de mi
61b3(mdo sde): ye shes mongs ma mchis// las dang las kyi rnam smin dong // rgyu yi shes pa gang lags pa// de dag thams cad ma lus par// 'jig rten rnam par 'dren pas ma khyen// du ma'i khams can 'gri/
61b4(mdo sde): rten dang // sna tshogs khams can des mkhyen to// khams mkhyen tshul la mkhas pa ste// 'jig rten gang zag zla ma mchis// mos pa sna tshogs ldan pa dang // de bzhin mos pa du ma can/ 'dzin
61b5(mdo sde): rten skyon medes mkhyen te// yang dag ji bzhin gzhan du min/ dbang po rtul po'ang rab tu mkhyen/ de bzhin dbang po'i bring yang mkhyen/ yongs smin dbang po des mkhyen te/ dbang po'i tshogs la dngang /
61b6(mdo sde): phyug go// thams cad du ni 'gro ba'i lam// yang dag ji bzhin des mkhyen te// mngon shes dbang po bsam gtan stobs// byang chub yan lag rnam thar mkhyen// kun nas nyon mongs rnam
61b7(mdo sde): byang dag / rnam par dgod pa'ang des mkhyen to// thogs med ye shes gzigs mnga' bas// de la thogs pa yongs ma mchis// sngon tshe dpag tu med pa dag/ rnam pa du mar de gzigs te// bdag dang /
62a1(mdo sde): gzhan gyi ma lus par// yang dag de bzhin du gzhan du min// de'i spyan ji ma mchis shing // mi'i las shin tu 'das pa ste// sems can shi' pa skyeb snapa/ des ni rje/
62a2(mdo sde): pasnga rab tu gzigs// zag pa bdang mkhyen pa ste// rnam par grol ba'ang rab tu mkhyen// rag med khams ni gang lags pa// de ni 'dren pas rab tu mkhyen// sangs rgyas mnga' chen sbyar ba yi// stobs bcu
62a3(mdo sde): 'di dag mtshungs ma mchis// sems gcig la ni kun nas kyang // sems la rtogs pa mi mnga' ste// blang med dor ba med tshul du// lhun gyis grub par de dag 'byung // sngar bskor 'khor lo'i shugs
62a4(mdo sde): bzhin du// rtog pa mi mnga' byung ba ste// sems can kun gyi rnam bsam pa// sems gcig gis ni rab tu mkhyen// 'on kyang sems dang sems can la// gnyis kyi blo ni mi 'byung ngo // de bas sangs
62a5(mdo sde): rgyas dbang sgyur la// skyon ni gang yang mi mnga' ste// chos rnams kun la mkhas pa de// yon tan dpal ni kun las 'phags// rgyal po chen po dge sbyong go'u ta ma de ni mi 'jigs pa bzhi dang ldan
62a6(mdo sde): pa'o// smras pa bram ze chen po dge sbyong go'u ta ma de mi 'jigase pa gang dag dang ldan pas/ mi 'jigs bzhi dang ldan pa zhes bya ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i mi 'jigs pa bzhi po de dag gang yin//
62a7(mdo sde): smras pa/ rgyal po chen po 'di la dge sbyong go'u ta ma de ni nga yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas so zhes bdag nyid dam bcas na/ chos 'di rnams khyod kyis mngon par rdzogs par sang ma rgyas so zhes lha dang
62b1(mdo sde): bcas pa/ bdud dang bcas pa/ tshangs pa dang bcas pa// dge sbyong dang rnam de'i skye dgu dang bcas pa'i 'jig rtenan nos dang 'thun par dag 'jig dug shol du hrI srung dag par rjes su smyig na
62b2(mdo sde): te/ rgyu de yang dag par rjes su ma gzigs pas/ bde ba brnyes shing mi 'jigs pa brnyes nas gnas te/ khyu mchog gi gnas su dam 'cha' zhing 'khor gyi nang du seng gi'i sgra yang dag par zlog la/
62b3(mdo sde): tshangs pa'i 'khor lo dge sbyong ngam/ bram ze'am/ gzhan su yang rung bas chos dang 'thun par 'jig rten du mi bskor ba bskor bar mdzad pa dang / nam de zag pa zad pa ste/ da ni zag pa zad do zhes bdag
62b4(mdo sde): nyid dam bcas na/ de la khyod kyis zag pa de dag ma zad do zhes lha dang bcas pa/ bdud dang bcas pa/ tshangs pa dang bcas pa/ dge sbyong dang bram ze'i skye dgu dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten na chos dang mthun
62b5(mdo sde): par 'ga' zhig bdag la rgol ba'i rgyu de yang dag par rjes su ma gzigs te/ rgyu de yang dag par rjes su ma gzigs pas/ bde ba brnyas shing mi 'jigs pa brnyes nas gnas te/ khyu mchog gi gnas
62b6(mdo sde): su dam 'cha' zhing / 'khor gyi nang du seng ge'i sgra yang dag par sgrog la/ tshangs pa'i 'khor lo dge sbyong ngam/ bram ze'am/ gzhan su yang rung bas chos dang 'thun par 'jig rten dum bskor ba bskor bar
62b7(mdo sde): mdzad pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pas gang dag par du gcod pa'i chos su gsungs pa de dag rten kyang bar du gcod par mi 'gyur ro zhes lha dang bcas pa/ bdud dang bcas pa tshangs pa dang bcas pa dge
63a1(mdo sde): sbyong dang bram ze'i skye dgu dang bcas pa'i 'jig rtenan chos dang rdzun par 'ga' zhig bdag 'argol ba'i rgyu de sang dag par rjes su mi ga gas te/ sang dag rjes sum ga sa
63a2(mdo sde): pas/ bde ba brnyes shing mi 'jigs pa brnyes nas gnas te/ khyu mchog gi gnas su dam 'chal zhing / 'khor gyi nang du seng ge'i sgra yang dag par klog la/ tshangs pa'i 'khor lo dge sbyong ngam/ bram ze'am/ gnan su/
63a3(mdo sde): yang rung bas chos dang 'thun par 'jig rten du ma bskor ba bskor bar mdzad pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pas 'phags pa nges par 'byin pa'i lam gang gsungs pa de bsten kyang yang dag par sdug bsngal zad par
63a4(mdo sde): rgyur mi 'gyur ro zhes lha dang bcas pa/ bdud dang bcas pa/ tshangs pa dang bcas pa/ dge sbyong dang bram ze'i skye dgu dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten na chos dang 'thun par 'ga' zhig bdag la rgol ba'i rgyu de yang
63a5(mdo sde): dag par rjes su mi gzigs te rgyu de yang dag par rjes su ma gzigs pas/ bde ba brnyes shing mi 'jigs pa brnyes nas gnas te/ khyu mchog gi gnas su dam 'cha' zhing / 'khor gyi nang du seng ge'i/
63a6(mdo sde): sgra yang dag par sgrog la/ tshangs pa'i 'khor lo dge sbyong ngam/ bram ze 'am/ gzhan su yang rung bas chos dang 'thun par 'jig rten du ma bskor ba bskor bar mdzad pa ste/ rgyal po chen po 'di dag
63a7(mdo sde): ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i mi 'jigs pa bzhi ste/ de dag dang ldan pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa ni 'khor gyi nang du seng ge'i sgra yang dag par sgrog ste/ de'i slad du de la skyon ma mchis lags so// de la 'di skad
63b1(mdo sde): ces kyi / dadang pargyang sa pa'i sems can ni// 'ga' med lhag pa ga la zhes/ mi yi 'dren pa 'khor ma smra/ seng ge'i spyan zlog par mdzad// nga'i chos rnams sangs rgyas hA/
63b2(mdo sde): gzhan du ma ni de gzigs rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas de// bsgrengs pa mi mnga' seng ge bzhin// la la de la rgol 'gyur ba'i// rgyu ni yang dge mi garigs te/ rgyu yang gzigs par mgyur pas// 'dren pa snod
63b3(mdo sde): pa mi mnga' sgrog zag pa thams cad zag gyur te// nga yi sku la zag pa med// de phyir lhar bcas 'jig rten na// nga dang mtshungs pa gang yang med// bar du gcod pa'i chos gang dag/ skye bo rnams langs bstan
63b4(mdo sde): pa/ de kun yang dag nyid du smras// gzhan du 'gyur ba yod ma yin// nges par 'byin pa'i chos gang dag/ ngas sangs rgyas nas rab bstan pa// chos rnams de dag bsten byas na// bar du gcod par 'gyurab
63b5(mdo sde): med/ de 'dra pa' bo chen pos mkhyen// de bzhin gshegs pas bde brnyes pas// 'jigs med pa'i brnyes gyur te// thub pa bsgrengs pa mi mngar bzhugs// sus kyang bskor bar ma gyur pa'i// tshangs
63b6(mdo sde): pa'i 'khor lo rab tu bskor// rkang gnyis dam pa ma gtogs par// 'jig rten dag na bskor mi nus// rgyal po chen po yang dge sbyong go'u ta ma do ni sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco/ brgyad po 'di
63b7(mdo sde): dag dang ldan pa'o// smras pa/ 'am me chen po dge sbyong go'u ta ma'i sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad pa de dag gang yin/ spros pa/ rgyal po chen po de la sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad
64a1(mdo sde): ni de bzhin gshegs pa la 'khrul pa mi mnga' ba dang / ca co mi mnga' ba dang / bsnyel ba mi mnga' ba dang / sems mnyam par ma bzhag pa mi mnga' ba dang shatha dad pa'i 'du shes/
64a2(mdo sde): mi mnga' ba dang / so sor ma brtags pa'i btang snyoms mi mnga' ba dang / 'dun pa nyams pa mi mnga' ba dang brtson 'grus nyams pa mi mnga' ba dang / dran pa nyams pa mi mnga' ba dang / ting nge 'dzin
64a3(mdo sde): nyams pa mi mnga' ba dang / shes rab nyams pa mi mnga' ba dang / rnam par grol ba nyams pa mi mnga' ba dang / lus kyi las thams cad ye shes sngon du 'gro zhing // ye shes kyi rjes su 'brang ba dang / ngag
64a4(mdo sde): gi lus thams cad ye shes sngon du 'gro zhing ye shes kyi rjes su 'brang ba dang / yid kyi las thams cad ye shes sngon du 'gro zhing / ye shes kyi rjes su 'brang ba dang / 'das pa'i dus la mchags mchog
64a5(mdo sde): pa'i ye shes mthong ba 'jug pa dang / ma 'ongs pa'i dus la mchags mthogs pa'i ye shes mthong ba 'jug pa dang da ltar gyi dus la mchags ma thogs pa'i ye shes mthong ba 'jug pa ste/ co brgyad po/
64a6(mdo sde): dag ni dge sbyong go rdu \u0f7f mda'i sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams te/ rgyal ba chen po bzhin gshegs pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad pa dag dang ldanapas// de'i srang du la tshun mam
64a7(mdo sde): lags so/ mas 'di skad ces bgyi/ sangs rgyas lani 'khrul mi mngag/ bzhin mi mang ste// de'i dgongs pa rnams mi mngag/ phyi kun rkyen tshun me sa ma da nga du ga so mams/
64b1(mdo sde): ste/ rnam par g.yeng ba'i drugs mi mngag// sa sor bcugs pa'i btang snyoms te/ 'dun pa nyams pa mi meda'a'o// de'i rtson 'grus cug tu 'bar// bsgyel mang bar 'gas te// shes rab dra ni rlom/
64b2(mdo sde): dang bzang po gzigs pa thams mi mngag// ye shes kyis kyang de mi 'khrugs// da yi lus dang ngag yid las// ye shes sngon du 'gro ba ste// ye shes kyin rjes su 'brang // ye shes 'dral ba ma mchis ti// dus/
64b3(mdo sde): pa'i dus la thogs ma mchis// ma 'ongs dus dang da ltar la'ang // de yi ye shes thogs ma mchis// dge sbyong bdag nyid che ba yi// de yi yon tan 'di 'dra bas// 'di las gzhan yang tshad med pa// bdag gis
64b4(mdo sde): bgrang ba'i rngo mi thog/ de nas rgyal po gtum po rab snang de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon tan dang che ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnam pa de lta bu dag thos nas/ tshim zhing mgul yi rangs te/ rab tu dga' nas dga' ba
64b5(mdo sde): dang / yid bde ba skyes te/ gcer bu pa'i bu bden smra la dad pa tshad med cing bsam gyis mi khyab pa skyes par gyur te/ ston pa'i 'du shes rnyed nas/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi 'du shes dang / byang chub ston
64b6(mdo sde): pa'i 'du shes dang / thams cad mkhyen par sgrol ba'i 'du shes dang yang dag par skul ba'i 'du shes dang / rjes su dran par byed pa'i 'du shes dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa bsam/
64b7(mdo sde): gyis mi khyab pa la gnas pa'i 'du shes kyang thob par gyur to// des 'du shes yid la bya ba de lta bu dang ldan pa'i sems kyis mu tig go 'phreng ba 'bum ri ba dang / rin zeng med pa'i ras bcos bu thugs su
65a1(mdo sde): gyur bas/ gcer busas smral rgyas kyi dag 'du phyir gnano// 'byud kyin du brjod pa du da/ ba sa na sa sa ya ra
65a2(mdo sde): legs par smras pa legs so legs so// bden sgra khyod kyis chos bstan pa 'din thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes dang 'thun pa'i rjes su 'thun pa'o// khyod kyi chos bstan pa 'du ni thams cad mkhyen pa nyid tho nga/
65a3(mdo sde): byed pa'o// khyod kyi chos bstan pa 'di ni 'khor 'byung bar byed pa'o// khyod kyis chos bskrun pa 'di ni nyon mongs pa'i dri ma rnams dag par byed pa'o// khyod kyis chos bstan pa 'di ni ser sna'i sgo glegs rnams 'jom
65a4(mdo sde): pa'o// khyod kyis chos bstan pa 'di ni gtong ba'i rnga rnams rdung bar byed pa'o// khyod kyis chos bstan pa 'di ni nga rgyal gyi ri rnams snyil bar byed pa'o// khyod kyis chos bstan pa 'di ni sred pa'i rgya mtsho skem par byed/
65a5(mdo sde): pa'o// khyod kyis chos bstan pa 'di ni mi shes pa'i thabs po snang bar byed pa'o// khyod kyis chos bstan pa 'di ni sems can yongs su smin par byed pa'i dus dang tshod las mi 'da' ba'o// de skad ces smras pa dang /
65a6(mdo sde): gcer bu pa'i bu bden smras/ rgyal po gtum po rab snang la 'di skad ces smras so// rgyal po chen po de de bzhin te/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod lam ni gang yang rung / sems can 'dul bar
65a7(mdo sde): mi 'gyur ba de gang yang ma mchis so// chos bstan pa gang yang rung / theg pa chen po dang mi mthun pa de gang yang ma mchis so// thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes yang dag pa mi sgrub pa de lta bu ma mchis so//
65b1(mdo sde): tsan mongs pa thams cad da par ma bgyid pa sa bum mangs so// 'khor ba'i nyes pa mthon pa des bum mchis so// mya ngan las 'das pami sgrub dres bya mas chis so// byung ru sems su /
65b2(mdo sde): dang mi mthun pa de lta bu ma mchis so// rgyal ba chen po byang chub sems dpa'i rtsom pa thams cad ni bdag gi don dang / gzhan gyi don dang / gnyis ka'i don yongs su grub par bgyid pa'o// gcer blo pa
65b3(mdo sde): bu bden smras bstan pa 'dri bshad pa'i tshe/ rgyal po gtum po rab snang gis phyir mi ldog pa'i dad pa thob par gyur to// rgyal bu gzhon nu bcu drug gis dga' ba'i shugs kyi yul zhes bya ba'i dad pa thob
65b4(mdo sde): bar gyur to// lha'i bu khri brgyad stong gis sangs rgyas kyi rgyan bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin thob par gyur to// rgyal po'i pho brang de'i mdang / gcer bu pa'i 'khor de'i nang nas mi khri sum stong ldan
65b5(mdo sde): med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems skyes par gyur te/ de dag thams cad kyis rang rang gi gos kyis gcer bu pa'i sa chos kyi dgab pa'i phyir bskon te/ 'di skad kyi tshig kyang brjod par/
65b6(mdo sde): gyur te/ bdag cag gis 'di ltar rigs kyi bu bden smra mthong zhing rjes su 'thun pa'i chos bstan pa 'di thos pa ni/ bdag cag gis rnyed pa legs par rnyed do zhes brjod nas/ 'di skad kyi tshig kyang
65b7(mdo sde): smras te/ bden sla tshur spyon/ dbacom ldan 'das de blta ba dang / de la phyag bya ba dang / bsnyen bkur bgyi ba'i phyir bcud do// de bzhin gshegs pa de ni bdag cag nyid kyi skyed mos tshal na
66a1(mdo sde): bdugs so// ba smras smras pa/ kyang chur sheg/ rgyal ba dang nas/ nga dang cas/ na nga sa/ song dal kyi ma dang cas/ 'khor gyi medang
66a2(mdo sde): par ldan cig 'thun par bgyis te/ bkod pa chen pos 'dong ngo // de nas rgyal po gtum po rab snang gis grong khyer thams cad du dril gyi sgra bsgrags te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gan du su mi 'gro ba da'i/
66a3(mdo sde): chad pa ni bsad pa'o zhes bsgo'o// de nas grong gi mo skyes pa dang / bud med dang / khye'u dang / bu mo thams cad kyis rgyal po gtum po rab snang gi bka' de thos nas me tog dang / spos dang /
66a4(mdo sde): me tog 'phreng dang / byug pa dang / sil snyan dang / pheg rnams thogs te/ grong khyer chen po 'phags rgyal gyi phyi rol du 'thon te/ skyed mos tshal du 'dong bar chas nas/ rgyal po gtum po rab
66a5(mdo sde): snang la sdod cing 'khod par gyur to// de nas rgyal po gtum po rab snang gcer bu pa'i bu bden smra dang lhan cig/ blon po'i tshogs dang lhan cig/ rgyal bu gzhon nu dang dpung gi tshogs dang lhan cig/ btsun//
66a6(mdo sde): mo'i 'khor dang lhan cig/ grong rdal ba'i mi dang / yul gyi mi rnams dang lhan cig/ 'khor gyi mi dang chab sgo ba rnams dang lhan cig tu thams cad kyis yongs su bskor cing / dpung gi bkod pa chen pos mdun
66a7(mdo sde): du bdar nas gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang ba dar dag ni bsgreng / sil snyan byed pa 'bum dag ni bun long du byas/ gar dang / glu dang / rol mo'i sgra dbyangs ni bsgrags ka rol mo'i spyad kim pa la dang /
66b1(mdo sde): nagul dang / lakhar ngad krol dang / reg gi smani bsngags/ rtadang glang po che rnams ni snga 'byin/ bkra shis kyi bum pa gser zag gis btags pa 'bum dag thogs pa rnams ni mdun du brtse ste/ glang po/
66b2(mdo sde): che'i shing rta pa rnams dang / rta'i shing rta pa rnams dang / srog chags 'bum phrag dgu bcu rtsa brgyad dang lhan cig tu rgyal po'i mthu chen po dang / rgyal po'i 'byor pa chen po dang / rgyal po'i rnam par 'brul
66b3(mdo sde): pa chen po dang / rgyal po'i rnam par rtseb chen pos rang gi skyed mos tshal ga la ba dang / bcom ldan 'das ga la ba der song ste phyin nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ lan gsum
66b4(mdo sde): bkor ba byas nas/ phyogs gcig tu 'dug go// gcer bu pa'i bu bden smra yang 'khor dang bcas te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal nas/ lan 'bum phrag du mar bskor ba
66b5(mdo sde): byas te/ thal mo sbyar nas mig mi 'dzums par bcom ldan 'das la lta zhing 'dug go/ de nas tshe dang ldan pa shA ri'i bus/ gcer bu pa'i bu bden smra bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan snga nas/ mig mi 'dzum/
66b6(mdo sde): par bcom ldan 'das la lta zhing 'dug pa mthong ngo // mthong nas kyang 'di snyam du sems te/ kye ma gcer bu pa'i bu bden smra 'di ci zhig 'dod de 'dir 'ongs snyam nas/ de ltar rnam par brtags/
66b7(mdo sde): te/ gcer bu pa'i bu bden smra la 'di skad ces smras so// bden smra khyod ci zhig 'dod de/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i thad du 'ongs ci bcom ldan 'das blta bar 'dod dam chos nyan
67a1(mdo sde): nas sa du sa smras/ sus smras

86a5(mdo sde): rgyan bkod pa gzhon nur gyur pa dang / lag na pad+ma dang / lag na rdo rje dang / nyi 'od dang / nor bu dang / glog dang / nyi ma dang / zla ba dang / brgya byin dang / tshangs pa thams cad zil gyis gnon pa'i//

86a7(mdo sde): ba'i blo gros dang / rdul med rnam par gnon dang / rnam dag rnam par gnon dang / phung po rnam par gnon dang / skye mched rnam par gnon dang / khams rnam par gnon dang / stong pa nyid rnamapas/

87b7(mdo sde): can thams cad kyi phyir sems bskyed cing byang chub rnam par 'tshang rgya ba dang ma bral ba sha stag go// thams cad kyang sems can gcig gi sems kyi dmigs pa la 'jug pas sems can ma lus pa thams
88a1(mdo sde): cad kyi sems kyi dmigs pa la mkhas pa dang ldan pa sha stag go// thams cad kyang rang byung gi ye shes kyi sa las ma bskyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i lus dang ldan pa gsu/

88a6(mdo sde): khyad par gyi bsam pa phun sum tshogs pa sha stag go/ thams cad kyang sangs rgyas 'byung ba thams cad kyi thad du 'gro zhing skul ba la mkhas pa sha stag go/ thams cad kyang de bzhin gshegs pa

88b1(mdo sde): 'jig rten khams su sangs rgyas 'byung ba kun tu ston par byed pa sha stag go/ thams cad kyang kun nas nyon mongs pa can gyi 'jig rten gyi khams yongs su sbyong bar byed pa sha stag go// thams cad
88b2(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi las kyi sgrib pa rgyun gcod par byed pa sha stag go/ thams cad kyang chos kyi dbyings sgrib pa med pa la zhugs pa sha stag go// thams cad kyang nam mkha'i khams

89a1(mdo sde): pa'i mdog yongs su 'grub pa'i gzugs la gnas pa sha stag go/ thams cad kyang skra tsam gyi khyon gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kun tu ston pa la mkhas pa sha

142a1(mdo sde): te/ den sprul pa mi bad pa shin tu sprin gyi bdag po zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa'o// yang skang rdo rje 'dus pa'i sgra ma lus pa ji nu'i rgya mtsho mching rnam sna
142a2(mdo sde): bar med na rin po che'i phur pa byas pa shin tu gong du 'phags pa zhes bya ba'i dri chu'i rgya mtsho mching rnam ste/ de na rin po che'i rgyal mtshan bsgreng ba zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rigs
142a3(mdo sde): rab tu gnas so// de'i bar med na me tog gi rgyal mtshan gyi snyoms par brgyan pa zhes bya ba'i dri chu'i rgya mtsho mching rnam ste/ de na snang ba thams cad ston pa zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams
142a4(mdo sde): kyi rigs rab tu gnas so// de'i bar med na rin po che'i gtso'i sprin can zhes bya ba'i dri chu'i rgya mtsho mching rnam ste/ de na rin po ni thams cad kyi 'og gi rgyan snang ba rnam par ldang ngo zhes bya ba'i
142a5(mdo sde): 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rigs rab tu gnas so// de'i bar med na rin po che'i sdong po ke sa ra'i kha dog rgyan ces bya ba'i ji nu'i rgya mtsho mching rnam ste/ de la legs par brtsegs pa gzi brjid
142a6(mdo sde): snyan gyi kong rgyan zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rigs rab tu gnas so// de'i bar mengan rin po che gtsa'i gos rab tu brgyan pa'i tshogs rgyan zhes bya ba'i ji chu'i rgya mtsho mching rnam ste/
142a7(mdo sde): de na rgya mtsho mching nam gyi snang ba zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rigs rab tu gnas so// de'i bar med na rin po che'i sdong ma yal ga brtsegs pa zhes bya ba'i 'jig cen
142b1(mdo sde): kyi khams kyi rgya mtsho mching rnams// don rin mche'i 'od 'gran sprin la rab tu gnas pa zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rigs rab tu gnas so// de'i bar med na 'du
142b2(mdo sde): 'og yang dag par ston pa zhes bya ba'i dri chu'i rgya mtsho mching rnam ste/ de na chags pa med pa'i rdo rje kun tu rjes su spyod pa zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rigs rab tu gnas so//
142b3(mdo sde): de'i bar med na kun tu pad+mo lngab lhub ces bya ba'i dri chu'i rgya mtsho mching rnam ste/ de na mtha' med pa'i 'gram rgya mtsho mching rnam 'khyil ba zhes bya ba 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rigs
142b4(mdo sde): rab tu gnas so// de'i bar med na rin po che dam pa'i yan lag lhab lhub ces bya ba'i dri chu'i rgya mtsho mching rnam ste// de na zhing gi 'og dmigs pa'i mdzod ces bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi kham/
142b5(mdo sde): kyi rigs rab tu gnas pa de lta bu la sogs pa brjod du med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi mchog tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa ji chu'i rgya mtsho mching rnam thams cad kyi phyi rol kho ra khor yug
142b6(mdo sde): gi mtshams na/ mi phigs pa'i snying po can zhes bya ba'i dri chu'i rgya mtsho mching rnam sa// de na pad+mo'i dkyil 'khor shin tu rnam par phye ba'i 'khor lo zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rigs
142b7(mdo sde): rab tu gnas te/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi stobs la 'jug pa'i sgra ma lus pa'i gzhi'o// der thams cad kyi 'og ma ni shin tu dri'i snying po zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams te/ de na tshad
143a1(mdo sde): med pa'i 'od sprul pa'i rgyal po zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa'o// 'jig rten gyi khams de'i rigs kyi dbus rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan gyi 'jig rten gyi khams kyi 'og
143a2(mdo sde): dang mnyam pa na/ bsam du med pa'i rgyan gyi tshul gyi sgo mo zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams te/ de na mi dkar ba'i ye shes tshangs pa zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa'o// de'i gong mi
143a3(mdo sde): mjed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams kyi 'og dang mnyam pa na/ phyogs kyi snang ba me tog gi snying po zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams te/ de na seng ge spyan 'od 'phro sprin zhes bya ba de bzhin
143a4(mdo sde): gshegs pa'o// de'i gong 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rigs kyi steng na// rgya mtsho mching rnam gyi sgra zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams te/ de na chu'i lha 'od 'phro zhal zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs
143a5(mdo sde): pa'o// yang lha'i grong khyer nor bu'i mkhar bu'i rgyan gyi ji chu'i rgya mtsho mching rnam ste/ de'i bar med na snang ba'i 'khor lo rnam par 'tsher ba zhes bya ba'i ji chu'i rgya mtsho mching rnam skye
143a6(mdo sde): de na brjod du med pa'i phyogs kyi gnas brgyan pa zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rigs rab tu gnas so// de'i bar med na rin po che'i rdul lam rnam par bris pa zhes bya ba'i dri chu'i rgyam
143a7(mdo sde): mching rnam ste// de na 'khyil ba du mar 'jug pa zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rigs rab tu gnas so// de'i bar med na rgyan thams cad snyoms par thar pa'i 'og ces bya ba'i
143b1(mdo sde): dri nu'i rgya mtsho mching rnam ste/ de na rin po che'i 'od rnam par snang ba zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rigs rab tu gnas so// de'i bar med na rin po cheng pa rnam pa'i cha 'dus pa zhes/
143b2(mdo sde): bya ba'i dri ru'i rgya mtsho mching rnam ste/ de na tshul gyi mtshams kyi mthu zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rigs rab tu gnas so// de'i bar med na rin po che'i rgyal mtshan gyi rtse mo'i
143b3(mdo sde): rgyan ces bya ba dri chu'i rgya mtsho mching rnam ste/ der 'jig rten gyi khams rnam par shes par byed pa// rgya mtsho mching rnam ma lus pa zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rigs rab tu
143b4(mdo sde): gnas so// de'i bar med na nyi ma'i khang pa yongs su sbyang bar snang ba zhes bya ba'i dri chu'i rgya mtsho mching rnam ste/ de na dbang po'i rnga ba kun tu 'thor ba la 'jug pa zhes bya ba'i 'jig
143b5(mdo sde): rten gyi khams kyi rigs rab tu gnas so// de'i bar med na sil khrol thams cad kyi skad bsgrags pa'i sgra yid du 'ong ba zhes bya ba ji chu'i rgya mtsho mching rnam ste/ de na 'khyil ba
143b6(mdo sde): thams cad kyi 'og tu 'jug pa zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rigs rab tu gnas so// de'i bar med na rgya mtshos spras pas rnam par bris pa zhes bya ba'i dri chu'i rgya mtsho mching rnam
143b7(mdo sde): ste/ de na 'od kyi sprin stug po dri ma med par 'bar ba zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rigs rab tu gnas so// de'i bar med na rin po che'i mar me'i 'od 'phro snyoms par
144a1(mdo sde): mngon du 'thor ba zhes bya ba'i dri chu'i rgya mtsho mching rnam ste/ de na sangs rgyas kyi smon lam sna tshogs kyi dbyibs byin gyi rlabs zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi kham/
144a2(mdo sde): kyi rigs rab tu gnas pa/ de lta bu la sogs pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med la/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi mchog tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i dri chu'i rgya mtsho mching rnam
144a3(mdo sde): ste/ thams cad kyi phyi rol kho ra khor yug gi mtshams na/ se mo do'i gos kyi tshogs zhes bya ba'i dri chu'i rgya mtsho mching rnam ste/ de na legs pa'i gos kun tu ston pa sprul pa zhes
144a4(mdo sde): bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rigs mngon la gong du 'phags pa 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar gyi sangs rgyas thams cad rnams kyi mtshan nyid kyi sgra ma lus pa ni
144a5(mdo sde): gzhi'o// der thams cad kyi 'og ma ni dbang po'i ke sar 'khyil ba'i snying po zhes bya ba'i dri chu'i rgya mtsho mching rnam ste/ de na rab tu grol bar dga' byed ces bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams
144a6(mdo sde): kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi mchog tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams mtha' gcig tu yongs su dag pa ni 'khor rnam/ de na sad pa'i ye shes pas mi 'jam pa
144a7(mdo sde): zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa'o// de'i gong sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i mchog tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams rnams las 'das la'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi
144b1(mdo sde): rigs kyi dbus rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan gyi 'jig rten gyi khams kyi 'og dang mnyam pa na/ rin po che'i dpal dra ba'i rgyu ma zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi sangs rgyas kyi ning bcu'i mchog/
144b2(mdo sde): za ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams mtha' gcig tu yongs su dag pa ni 'khor rnams te/ de na tshad med pa'i glog gi gtso/ drang srong chen po zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa
144b3(mdo sde): de'i gong sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi mchog tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams rnams las 'das pa'i mi mjed pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi 'og dang mnyam pa na/ rin po che'i sgrar
144b4(mdo sde): pad+mo seng ge zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i mchog tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams kun tu nyon mongs pa dang / rnam par dag pa ni 'khor
144b5(mdo sde): rnams te/ de na dri ma med pa'i drag shul thos pa thogs pa med pa zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs la'o// de'i gong sangs rgyas kyi zhing bdun gyi mchog tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i 'jig rten gyi
144b6(mdo sde): khams rnams las 'das pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rigs kyi gong na/ rin po che'i klu 'od kyi kha dog ces bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing nyi shu'i mchog tu phra ba'i rdul dang
144b7(mdo sde): mnyam pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams mtha' gcig tu yongs su dag pa ni 'khor rnams te/ de na chos kyi khams yongs su rgyas pa rnam par snang mdzad ces bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa'o// kye rgyal
145a1(mdo sde): ba'i bu rnams sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med la bcu'i mchog tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i dri chu'i rgya mtsho mching rnam ste/ de dag la sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod
145a2(mdo sde): du med pa bcu'i mchog tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rigs rab tu gnas so// 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rigs de dag thams cad kyang / dri chu'i rgya mtsho mching
145a3(mdo sde): rnam de dag rnams la/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi lus rnam par shes par byed pa brnyan mar snang brgyal mtshar nor bu'i rgyal pos rab tu brgyan pa'i rgyan pad+mor rab tu gnas pa
145a4(mdo sde): ri/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rigs par med kyi mtshams gzhan dang gzhan pa'i rgyan rnams dang / gzhan dang gzhan pa'i rin po che'i kha dog gi snang ba rab tu btang ba'i rnams dang / gzhan
145a5(mdo sde): dang gzhan pa'i 'od zer gyi 'od dkyil 'khor gyi sprin gyis kun tu g.yogs pa'i rnams dang / gzhan dang gzhan pas brgyan pa'i rgyan gyi 'od rnams dang // gzhan dang gzhan pa'i bskal pa'i/
145a6(mdo sde): grangs kyi tshul bshad pa'i rnams dang / gzhan dang gzhan pa'i sangs rgyas kyi 'byung bar 'jug pa'i rnams dang / gzhan dang gzhan pa'i rgya mtsho mching rnam sgrog pa'i rnams dang // gzhan
145a7(mdo sde): dang gzhan pa'i sems can gyi lus yongs su rgyas pa'i rnams dang gzhan dang gzhan pa'i phyogs su 'jug pa tha mi dad pa'i rnams dang / gzhan dang gzhan pa'i sangs rgyas kyi rnam par sprul
145b1(mdo sde): bde bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi rlabs dang / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rigs re re nas kyang 'jig rten gyi mtshams rab tu btang ba dang / 'jig rten gyi dra ba dang / rgyan rab tu gnas pa thams cad/
145b2(mdo sde): kyis me tog 'og gi snying po rgyan gyi brgyan 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho mching rnam thams cad ji snyed pa 'jig rten gyi khams sna tshogs kyi tshul gyis kun tu rgyus so// 'jig rten gyi khams kyi
145b3(mdo sde): rigs gcig nas ji bzhin pa de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rigs thams cad kyis 'jig rten gyi khams kyi mtshams kyi sgo thams cad kyis brgyan sna tshogs gnas pas 'jig rten gyi khams
145b4(mdo sde): kyi dra ba sna tshogs kyis me tog 'og gi snying po rgyan 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgya mtsho mching rnam thams cad ji snyed pa kun tu rgyas so// de nas yang kun tu bzang po byang chub sems dpas
145b5(mdo sde): lhag pa'i tshad du 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rigs mtha' dang dbus med pa 'jig rten gyi khyon gyi tshul gyi chad pa de nyid snang bar byed pa na/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par
145b6(mdo sde): bltas nas/ de'i tshon tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// 'jig rten khams kyi rgya mtsho ni// chos kyi khams dang tha me dang // yangs pa yangs par bris pa ni// nam mkha'i 'og tu
145b7(mdo sde): gnas pa'o// 'jig rten khams kyi rgya mtsho der// zhing gi rigs ni bsam med pa// rnam par gnas pa tha dad med// gzhan dang gzhan pa'i rnam sprul pa'o// rnam char 'dug pa dris pa ni//
146a1(mdo sde): sna tshogs kha dog rab tu gnas// zhing gi rigs rang rud pa ni// 'jig rten khams kyi rgya mtsho ru'o// sna tshogs lus kyis sgra ma lus// sangs rgyas rnam
146a2(mdo sde): sprul thams cad las// zhing gi rigs rnams sdang ba ni// las kyis shin tu rnam bris pa'o// lhun po rgya mtsho dra ba yang // 'khor lo 'khyil pa dkyil 'khor te// dal bcu rdul yangs
146a3(mdo sde): dbyibs// de dag gis ni de dag bskor// tshul khrims rgyal mtshan brtsegs pa dang // bsgyur ba rdo rje'i gnas pa rnams// bsam du med pa'i khyon rnams kyis// de dag rigs rnams
146a4(mdo sde): bskor ba'o// 'od kyi dra ba bsam med kyis// snang ba rgya mtsho btang bas ni// zhing gi rigs rnams 'bar ba yang // thams cad pad+mo rab tu gnas// re re'i yang ni rigs las
146a5(mdo sde): su 'od zer dra bas bsam med pa// 'od zer zhing du gyur nas su// rgyu'o phyogs kyi rgya mtsho ru// thams cad zhing gi rigs rnams kyi// dmigs pa thams cad sgo mo ru// tha/
146a6(mdo sde): cad tshul gyi 'jug pa yang // zad pa med pa'i tshul ni snang // bsam du med pa'i zhing rnams su// zad pa med pa'i rigs rnams 'byung // sna tshogs rgyan gyi bshad pa ni// drang srong chen
146a7(mdo sde): po'i byin rlobs so// zhing gi rigs ni de dag tu// 'jig rten khams ni bsam med de// gong bar 'gyur ba skye ba dang // kun tu 'byung dang mi 'byung ngo // ji bzhin shin tu lo ma rnams//
146b1(mdo sde): 'byung ba dang ni ltung ba yang // de ltar de bzhin zhing rigs su// 'jig rten khams rnams 'byung ba'o// ji ltar shing rnams snying po ru// 'bras bu rnam pa sna tshogs 'gyur/ de ltar/
146b2(mdo sde): de bzhin zhing rigs su// gon 'dun sems can 'byung ba'o// ji bzhin yang ni bye brag gis// 'bras bu snang ba sna tshogs par// de ltar las kyang bye brag gis// sems can
146b3(mdo sde): rnams kyi zhing byung ngo // ji ltar bsam rgyal rin chen ni// kha dog kun gyi snang ba ste// sems can bsam pa rnam dag phyir// de bzhin zhing rnams mthong ba'o// ji bzhin klu yi
146b4(mdo sde): rgyal pos sprin// nam mkha'i 'og tu stor byed pa// de ltar sangs rgyas smon lam gyis// sangs rgyas zhing rnams 'byung ba'o// sgyu ma byed pa'i sngags kyis su// rnam pa sna tshogs
146b5(mdo sde): bzhin ston pa// de bzhin sems can las kyis su// bsam med zhing rnams 'gyur ba'o// ji bzhin bris byas kyi ni gzugs// ri mo mkhan gyis ri mo bris// de ltar 'di dag
146b6(mdo sde): thams cad zhing // sems kyis shin tu bri bar bris// sems can rnams kyi gon 'dun lus// ji bzhin sems kyis brtags pa pa// de bzhin zhing rnams gon 'dun par//
146b7(mdo sde): thams cad las kyis bris pa'o// gzhan dang gzhan pa'i gzugs su ni// ji ltar snang ba 'dren pa rnams// ji bzhin sems can bsam pa la// de bzhin ning rnams mthong ba'o// pad+mo'i
147a1(mdo sde): dra ba phyi rol dang // sems can zhing rnams mtshams su ste// gzhan pa'i dbyibs dang kha dog rnams// bris par snang ba dri med pa'o// pad+mo dra ba de dag la'ang //
147a2(mdo sde): zhing gi dra ba rab tu gnas// rgyan sna tshogs su chad pa ni// sems can gon 'dun rnams kyi gnas// kha cig zhing gi de dag 'og/ kun tu nyon mongs pa ru gnas// sems
147a3(mdo sde): can rnams ni nyon mongs par// de dag tu ni chos nyid snang // bsam du med pa'i zhing rigs rnams// kun tu nyon mongs rnams dag kyang // sems can bsam pa
147a4(mdo sde): 'byung ba ru// byang chub sems dpa' rab tu gnas// kha cig zhing 'og mang po ni// rnam par dag dang nyon mongs yang // las kyi rgya mtsho su ni 'byung // byang chub sems/
147a5(mdo sde): dpe' rnams kyis sprul// kha cig zhing gis 'og btang ba// dri med cing ni rin chen gyi// rnam par bris pa dri med dag/ sangs rgyas kyis kyang yongs sbyangs so// zhing gi rigs ni
147a6(mdo sde): gcig tu yang // bskal pas bsreg pa bsam med pa// nyon mongs rnams la ston pa ste// zhing gi dkyil 'khor rab tu sra// rlung gi phung po smon lam gyis// chu'i phung rab tu gnas
147a7(mdo sde): pa ni// zhing rnams mang po byung bar 'gyur// sems can rnams kyi las bsag pas// lto shig zhing du gzhan gzhan pa// snang ba zhing gi chos nyid ni// de dag rnams ni 'byung min/
147b1(mdo sde): dang // de dag rnams cang ldog med do/ mang bzhing rnams 'byung ba ni// thams cad sems kyi sa tsugs// sangs rgyas byin gyi rlabs kyis ni// byin tu dag pa'i med sa
147b2(mdo sde): sa chen po yi zhing rnams ni/ kha cig byung ba sra ba'i rnams// snang ba med cing 'od med rnams// sdig pa'i las kyi gnas rnams so// kha cig ning ni rdo rje yi// kun tu nyon mongs
147b3(mdo sde): 'jigs pa che// 'de ba chung zhing sdug bsngal mang // bsod nams chung ba rnams kyi gnas// kha cig zhing rnams lcags kyi ste// zangs dang 'khar bar gnas pa rnams// sdig san/
147b4(mdo sde): las kyis khyab pa ni// nyam ji yi ri rnams so// 'jig rten de ru dmyal ba ste// sems can rnams ni mgon med sdug bsngal ba/ mun pa rgyud du thob pa ni// 'od 'phro'i rgya mtsho' bar/
147b5(mdo sde): ba'o// de bzhin byol song 'gro ba yang // bdag gi lus ni thag zug pa// rang gi lus kyis nyes pas na// sdug bsngal tshor ba'i tshor ba'o// snang ba gshin rje'i 'jig rten du// skom/
147b6(mdo sde): dang thubs nyon mongs pa// me yi ri la 'dzegs pa rnams// sdug bsngal tshor 'tshor ba'o// kha cig rin chen bdun rnams te// kha cig gnas ni rnam par bris// dge ba'i 'as
147b7(mdo sde): kyis byung ba'i rnams// rnam par bri bar khang pa brgyan// kha cig lnga dang mi rnams yang // mtho ris 'jig rten du ni ltos// dge ba'i bsod nams 'bras bus ldan// dge ba'i/
148a1(mdo sde): bde ba myong ba'o// nyag ma gcig gi rtse mor ni// bye ba zhing ni bsam med pa// sna tshogs rnam par bris pa'i dbyibs// de dag la yang 'dres pa med//
148a2(mdo sde): bdag bdag kun gyi las kyis su// sems can khams ni bsam med pa// sna tshogs 'du shes zin pa rnams// bde dang sdug bsngal myong ba'o// kha cig zhing ni mtha' med snang//
148a3(mdo sde): sems can thams cad gnas kyi gnas// rdo rje ut+pal 'byung ba'i rnams// bris pa dag pa dri med pa'o// zhing ni kha cig 'od zer gyi// 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rnams la gnas/
148a4(mdo sde): gser dang tsan dan las ni byung // 'od 'gro'i sprin dang mtshungs pa'o// nyi ma dkyil 'khor gyi ni zhing // dri yi gos kyis g.yogs pa dang // gzhan ni pad+mo'i gcig gis ni//
148a5(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rgyas// la lar mtshan nyid kha dog snang // zhing rnams rin chen brtsigs pas ni// dbang po'i dra bas 'od btang ba// 'od zer dra bas 'tsher ba'o//
148a6(mdo sde): rdo rje pad+mo kha cig ni// zhing rnams pog la gnas pa ste// gzhan ni nor bu brnyan mar snang // lto shig zhing ni rnam dag pa// me tog 'khyil bar byung ba rnams// lho shig zhing rnam bsam
148a7(mdo sde): med pa// sangs rgyas sprul pas kun tu g.yogs// byang chub sems dpa'i 'od dang mnyam// kha cig me tog shing rnams kyis// yal ga'i dkyil 'khor rnam par bris// nor bu'i
148b1(mdo sde): sprin ni kun tu 'bab// dkyil 'khor zhing gi rnam dag pa'o// rdo rje pad+ma'i zhing rnams ni// legs pa'i pad+mo ljang nge ste// sangs rgyas sprul pa snga ma lus// zhing gi dra babs ma med pang/
148b2(mdo sde): nor bu'i cod pan bris pa'i rnams// byang chub sems dpas brgyan pa ste// kha cig bstan par byung ba ni// rab tu btang bas sprul 'od do// sna tshogs tsan dan phye ma rnams// srin
148b3(mdo sde): mtshams spu yi lhang nge 'od// sangs rgyas thams cad 'od zer gyis// zhing gi 'byung ba zer ba'o// kha cig rgyan gyis snang ba'i rnams// zhing ni dri med snang ba ste// kha cig rgyan ni thams
148b4(mdo sde): cad kyis// rnam par bris par brgyan pa'o// kha cig zhing bcu rnams kyi ni// rgyan gyis su ni brgyan pa ste// gzhan zhing stong phrag du ma'i rnams// rgyan la rab tu gnas pa'o// zhing gi rgyan
148b5(mdo sde): ni bye bas su// kha cig zhing ni rnam par byis// sna tshogs rgyan gyi dbyibs pa rnams// bris par snang ba mthong ba'o// brjod du med pa'i zhing rnams na// rgyan ni gcig pu snang ba ste// gzhan
148b6(mdo sde): dang gzhan pa'i 'od btang ba// byung po sangs rgyas smon lam gyis// smon lam rgya mtsho mching rnam gyis// kha cig zhing rnams rnam par sbyangs// de dag thams cad rgyan du ni// zhing gi rgya ma
148b7(mdo sde): snang ba'o// kun tu bzang po smon lam gyis// zhing gang yongs su sbyangs pa ni// dus gsum zhing rnams de dag gi/ rgyan ni thams cad snang ba'o// rgyal ba'i bu ge ltos shig kye// zhing gi rigs su rnam
149a1(mdo sde): sprul pa// gang na zhin ni ma 'ongs rnams// rmi lam 'dra bar snang ba'o// ji snyed phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten du// 'das pa'i zhing gi rgya mtsho rnams// zhing gcig tu ni lhas/
149a2(mdo sde): shig dang // brnyan mar snang bar shin tu sprul// dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// zhing gi rnam sprul ji snyed pa// zhing gi rigs su snang ba ni// thams cad nang du chud par
149a3(mdo sde): 'dug pa'o// myos shig rdul gyi thog ma ru// sangs rgyas kun gyi rnam spangs pa// rgud par snang ba de dag la// mtshan ma med pa brnyan mar snang // kha cig rgya mtsho mching rnam
149a4(mdo sde): dbyibs// zhing gi rigs rnams mang po ltos// dbyibs ni lhun po ri yi rnams// 'jig rten khams ni bsam med pa'o// kha cig zhing ni shing tu brgyus// dbang po'i dra ba shin//
149a5(mdo sde): tu gnas// zhing gi dbyibs su shin tu bris// thams cad sangs rgyas kyis ni rgyas// nor bu'i 'khor lor gnas pa'i zhing // gzhan ni pad+mor gnas pa ste// cha brgyad du mar dris
149a6(mdo sde): pa'i rnams// kha dog sna tshogs shin tu dri med pa'o// stan gyi dbyibs su kha cig dang // gle ba mkhar gyi dbyibs su ste// dga' ru'i dbyibs pa kha cig ni// tshangs pa'i lus su
149a7(mdo sde): shin tu gnas// lha yi dbang po gtsug gi dbyibs// zla ba kham par gnas pa'i rnams// nor bu ri yi dbyibs pa ni// nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor du ni gnas pa'o// dri chu mtsho ni 'khyil
149b1(mdo sde): ba rnams// 'jig rten khams ni shin tu gnas// 'od zer dkyil 'khor gyen dbyibs// spun ni sangs rgyas mngon par sbyangs// 'khor lo bde bar byed pa'i dbyibs// 'jig rten ma/

149b3(mdo sde): ste/ 'od 'phro ri yi dbyibs gnas pa// byang chub sems dpas rgyas pa'o// zhing rnams rnams ni seng ge dbyibs// nor bu'i go char gnas pa yang // du ma'i gzug

149b5(mdo sde): smon pas byung ba'o// kha cig zhing ni bskal par mnyam// gzhan ni bskal pa bcu pa ste// kha cig zhing ni rdul dang mtshungs// bskal pa bye bar bsgrags pa'o// kha cig

150a1(mdo sde): sangs rgyas sprul pa 'ongs nas su// rnam par sprul pa ston pa'o// 'da' ba'i tshe la shi 'phos par// sangs rgyas byang chub rnam par sad// bdud kyi sde ni
150a2(mdo sde): bsnyil nas su// chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'o// sems can rnams kyi bsam pa ji bzhin par// sna tshogs gzugs su ston pa ni// 'jig rten kun tu tha mi dang // chos kyi 'khor/

150a4(mdo sde): rgyas ltar ni mi ster te// de nyid gcig tu kun tu yang // sangs rgyas bsam las mthong ba'o// sangs rgyas zhing ni re re na// sangs rgyas bye ba bsam med pa// de ru rgyal ba byung ba
150a5(mdo sde): ste/ gang zhing sangs rgyas mang ba na'o// rgyal ba re re de ru ni// sprul pa mang po mthong zhing ni// chos kyi khams ni rgyas nas su// sems can rgya mtsho gdul bar mdzad//

150b1(mdo sde): mthong ba/ sems can rnams kyi bsod nams 'byung // ri yi snang bar yod pa dang // kha cig zhing na nor bu'i 'od// me mar snang ba gzhan du ni// sems can rnams kyi las/
150b2(mdo sde): kyis byang // kha cig zhing du sangs rgyas 'od// byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rgyas// pad+mo'i 'od zer 'od kyi zhing // 'od 'phro'i sdung ba mdzes pa'o// me tog snang ba'i

150b4(mdo sde): chas snang bar byas// sangs rgyas byin gyi rlabs kyis snang ba ni// sgra yid 'ong ba'i dbyangs snyan no// nor bu'i cod pan 'od snang dang // rdo rje gser gyi 'od 'phro 'tsher/

150b6(mdo sde): rnams kyis ni snang bar byas// sangs rgyas sbrul gyi snang ba dang // sangs rgyas sprin gyis mngon par g.yogs// kun tu 'od kyi snang ba ni// chos kyi khams dang mnyam

151a1(mdo sde): byol song rigs kyi dang // gshin rje'i 'jig rten sdug bsngal gang // kun tu nyon mongs ning du ni// mya ngan smos su rgya mtsho zer// kha cig tu ni//

151b3(mdo sde): pha rol na/ phyogs kun tu mig dri ma med pa rab tu snang ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho mching rnam gyi dbus na/ dpal gyi sgra zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams rnams yod par gyur/

151b5(mdo sde): pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams rnam par dag pa dang / kun tu snyoms pa ni 'khor rnams te/ kun tu zlum po dang / mtha' med pa'i rgyan gyis 'og brgyan pa dang / nor

151b7(mdo sde): snang ba/ ri rab lta bur grong khyer dang / khang pa'i rgyan te/ zas dang / skom dang / gos gang longs spyod yid du 'ong ba dang / gang tshogs su brtag par brgyan pa bshad do//
152a1(mdo sde): yang dpal sgra'i 'jig rten gyi khams de'i dbus na/ rnam par dag par snang ba zhes bya ba'i dri chu'i rgya mtsho mching rnam ste/ de ni me tog gi 'od 'phro dang mnyam

152a3(mdo sde): tog rgyas pa yal ga'i dkyil 'khor zhes bya ba stug po'i tshal chen po de/ dri'i rgyal mtshan stong phrag dpag tu med pa'i rnams bsgrengs pa'i rgyan dang / dpag tu med pa'i

152a7(mdo sde): 'phro'i sprin rnams kyis snang bar byas so// sems can gon 'dun gyi gnas rnams rin po che'i grong khyer bye ba ther 'bum brgya stong phrag bcus bskor ba na/ gang 'di nor bu'i yal ga'i

155a2(mdo sde): bcom ldan 'das yon tan thams cad kyi ri/ lhun po dpal gyi sprin de bzhin gshegs pa de pad+mo chen po der byung ba/ de bzhin nyid dang / mnyam pa nyid dang / chos kyi khams kyis rgyas pa'i sku ste/ sangs
155a3(mdo sde): rgyas thams cad kyi zhing skye bar mched pa dang / byang chub kyi dkyil thams cad du bzhugs pa'i sku dang / mtha' dang dpung med pa'i gzugs kyi sku shin tu rnam par dag pa dang
155a4(mdo sde): 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad shin tu gong du 'phags pa'i zil gyis mnan pa dang / mtshan nyid rin po che thams cad rgyas pa dang / sems can gyi gnas thams cad du snang ba byin

155b1(mdo sde): po ni sangs rgyas kyi gdan la bzhugs pa/ de bzhin du thams cad dang ldan pa'i sgra dpal gyi 'jig rten gyi khams kyi ri rab bye ba stong phrag drug cuH brgyad kyi ri rab spyi bo na bzhugs/
155b2(mdo sde): par snang ngo // de bzhin du kun tu mig dri ma med par snang ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgya mtsho mching rnam thams cad na/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i mchog tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i

155b5(mdo sde): sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i mchog tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i 'od zer 'khor rnams dang / rab tu btang nas 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rgyas te/ gdul ba thams cad rnams la skul

155b7(mdo sde): pa thams cad kyi tsha ba rnams nye bar zhi'o// sgrib pa thams cad kyi dra ba bsal ba/ sangs rgyas blta bar bsgrib pa'i ri rnams gtor to// sems can thams cad kyi rnyog pa rnams rnam par
156a1(mdo sde): sbyangs so// dge ba thams cad kyi rtsa ba'i rgya mtsho mching rnam rnams byung ngo // mos pa'i dkyil 'khor rgya che ba'i rnams yongs su sbyangs so// khom pa med pa thams
156a2(mdo sde): cad dang / ngan song dang / 'gro ba ngan la dang / g.yang sa'i 'jigs pa rnams dang bral lo// lus dang sems las byung ba rnams kyi gnod pa thams cad rab tu zhi nas/ sangs rgyas blta bar

156a7(mdo sde): nus sangs rgyas kyi rnam par sprul pa mthong nas/ sngon gyi dge ba'i rtsa ba byung bas chos bcu rnams skyes so// bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas thams cad yon tan gyi dkyil

157a1(mdo sde): ji rnyed pa la tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag sbas so// nyi ma'i sprin ni stong khrag rnams// nam mkhar shar baji bzhin pa// sangs rgyas kyi ni snang ba ni/

157b1(mdo sde): sprin rnams rgyal ba'i spyan sngar ro// byang chub dkyil du klog pa ni/ A yi rgya mtsho zab ma ste// sems can kun gyi sdug bsngal ni// ltos shig sangs rgyas rnam sprul lo// thams cad
157b2(mdo sde): rimathor bcus gyur to// dga' ba skyes nas shin tu dga'// 'jig rten mgon mar 'dang bar bya/ chos kyi rgyal po bltar 'phyir// ce rgyal ba'i bu rnams ga'i brjid che ba'i rgyal na
157b3(mdo sde): gzhon nu de tshigasu bcad 'di dag smra ba na/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis// sgra dpal gyi 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi sems can gyi gnas su rjes su klog go

157b7(mdo sde): bcas par// deng zhig rgyal ba blta ba ru// rgyan par gyis shig grong khyer ni// rgyan gyis su ni kun tu ste// glengs shig rgyal mtshan rtse mo rnams// sna tshogs nor bus rnam bris
158a1(mdo sde): pa'o// rin chen dra ba'i bla re rnams// bris shig nam mkha'i 'og tu ste// dkrob zhig sil khrol sprin rnams ni// nam mkha' 'di yi kun tu'o//
158a2(mdo sde): lam dang srang rnams brgyan nas su// rin chen gos rnams char du phob// theg pa rin chen rnams ni sbyor// 'der ngo rgyal ba lta ba ru// rang rang gi ni

158b1(mdo sde): babud med stong phrag sum cu rtsa bdun rnams dang / gzi brjid chen po la sogs pa gzhon nu lnga brgya rnams dang / blo gros kyi stobs la sogs pa blun pa stong phrag drug cu rnams

210b1(mdo sde): de la bdag ni bcom ma mchis te// des na gang zag mchog des bdag lung bstan// nam mkha' bar snang ji ltar bya rjes// de dgra ma mchis ma byung 'byung mi 'gyur// rgyal bas
210b2(mdo sde): bstan pa de bzhin mthong bas na// de na gang zag mchog gis bdag lung bstan// chos 'di thams cad nam mkha' bar snang bzhin// de rnams gang la'ang mngon par chags ma
210b3(mdo sde): mchis// phyogs nas mchis shing gang du'ang mchis ma mchis// des na gang zag mchog gis bdag lung bstan// ji ltar rmi lam na ni skom pa'i mis// chu grang dang bde
210b4(mdo sde): yis 'tshal na yang // skom pa chad cing zhi bar mi 'gyur ba// de bzhin bdag gis 'dod pa'i yon tan rtogs// rnga brdungs de la sa snga rnams rab 'byung ste// skye bo byis pa rnams
210b5(mdo sde): ni dga' bar gyur// de yang kod dang ni shing las kyang // ska de mi rnyed de bzhin chos nyid do// ji ltar pi lung len pa sbrengs pa yi// rgyud las sbyin pa'i sgra yang shin tu gtong/
210b6(mdo sde): shing dang drud rnams las kyang ma lags te// s+yA de mi rnyed de bzhin chos nyid do// gzugs dang skra dang ro dang ji rig kyang // pi lang dag gi sgra 'drar mthong bas na// btsam
210b7(mdo sde): dogs pa thams cad kun tu bcom// debs 'jig rten 'dren pas bdag lung bstan/ sa dang shing dang mun dpal bar // de bzhin 'das chu dang chur brten te// par snang bachen /
211a1(mdo sde): dag kun bskor nas// 'jig rten kun rdzob khyim du gyur ces brjod// de bzhin rus pa sen mo rgyus lpags dang // spu dang skra dang khrag rnam pags pa yis/
211a2(mdo sde): nam mkha' dag kyang kun nas bskor nas ni// de bzhin kun rdzob lus su gyur ces brjod// gzugs ni dbu ba 'dra ste snying po med// tshor ba rnams ni chu yi chu bur 'dra// 'du shes
211a3(mdo sde): rnams ni smig rgyu 'dra bar mthong // de la byis pa'i rang bzhin skye bos nor// sems pa dag ni chu shing snying po 'dra// rnam shes rnam pa kun tu sgyu ma bzhin// gang gis 'gro ba
211a4(mdo sde): lhar bcas 'khyam byas pa// de ltar mthong bas rgyal bas lung yang bstan/ de nas dge slong sprin gyi rgyal po des de bzhin gshegs pa mtshungs pa med pa'i gzi brjid 'od de la
211a5(mdo sde): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang ldan pa'i tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gis mngon par bstod nas/ dge ba'i rtsa ba des bskal pa brjod du med par nams kyang chos la rmongs par 'gyur//
211a6(mdo sde): nams kyang tshul khrims la snying por 'du shes par ma gyur/ ting nge 'dzin rnams la snying por 'du shes par mgyurate/ rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la gnam
211a7(mdo sde): bar gyur to// nams kyang shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la dngos por ma dmigs te/ 'di lta ste dper na/ mi zhig gzings las rgya mtsho chen po 'argal nas/ gzings bor te gar
211b1(mdo sde): dga' bar 'gro ba de bzhin du/ dge slong sbyin gyi rgyal 'a yang shes rab kyi ma rol tu phyin pa shes par byed mod kyi/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la mngon pa zhen par ma byed do// 'dri/
211b2(mdo sde): lta ste dper na/ mi zhig me 'dod pa rims dgos pa byed mod kyi/ tshig pa'i nyes pa yang srung ba de bzhin du/ byang chub sems dpa' sprin gyi rgyal po de yang shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pas chos
211b3(mdo sde): thams cad mthong mod kyi/ mngon par zhen pa'i nyes pa'ang srung ngo // shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa gzhan la'ang ston mod kyi/ mngon par zhen pa'i nyes pa las kyang zlog par byed
211b4(mdo sde): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pas sangs rgyas kyi zhing tshad med par sangs rgyas kyi bya ba byed mod kyi/ des sems can de dag dang sangs rgyas de dag tu 'dzin pa yang med do//
211b5(mdo sde): 'jam dpal de ji snyam du sems/ de'i tshe de'i dus na dge slong sprin gyi rgyal po zhes bya bar gyur pa de gzhan zhig yin pa snyam du 'dzin na/ 'jam dpal khyod kyis de ltar mi blta'o//
211b6(mdo sde): de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de bzhin gshegs pa don thams cad grub pa de/ de'i tshe de'i dus na dge slong sprin gyi rgyal po zhes bya bar gyur to// 'jam dpal de lta bas na thabs mkhas pa
211b7(mdo sde): gang dang ldan pas dge slong sprin gyi rgyal po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i thabs mkhas pa de dang ldan par byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos shes rab kyi pha rol tu
212a1(mdo sde): phyin pa la smad par bya'o// de la bu'i thabs mkhas pa dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni sangs rgyas kyi gang dpag tu med pa yongs su sbyong ngo // sangs rgyas/
212a2(mdo sde): kyi zhing grangs med/ bsam gyis mi khyab mtshungs pa med/ gzhal du med/ brjod du med pa yongs su sbyong ngo // de nas yang bcom ldan 'das kyis 'jam
212a3(mdo sde): dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la bka' stsal pa/ 'jam dpal de bzhin gshegs pa don thams cad grub pade sngon byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod pa na/ byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge
212a4(mdo sde): 'dzin zhi ba zhes bya ba bsgoms te/ rab tu goms par byas/ lam du byas/ rten du byas/ nan tan du byas/ rab tu 'dris par byas/ legs par brtsams shing rab tu rdzogs
212a5(mdo sde): par byas te/ des sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa zhi ba dang rab tu zhi bar rtogs so// tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang / bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa dang / brtson 'grus kyi
212a6(mdo sde): pha rol tu phyin pa dang / bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yang zhi ba dang / rab tu zhi bar rtogs so// 'di lta ste dper na'adus ma byas kyi khams
212a7(mdo sde): zhi ba dang / rab tu zhi ba de bzhin du/ pha rol tu phyin pa drug kyang zhi ba dang rab tu zhi bar rtogs so// 'di lta ste dper na 'dus byas kyi khams mi skye mi 'gag pa de bzhin du/ pha rol
212b1(mdo sde): tu phyin pa drug kyang mi skye mi 'gag go/ 'di sa se per na 'dug thams cad kyi thams cad du mi dmigs pa de bzhin du darol tu phyin pa drug kyang thams cad kyi thams cad du mi dmis/
212b2(mdo sde): te/ pha rol tu phyin pa drug ji lta ba bzhin du chos thams cad kyang mi skye mi 'gag go// chos thams cad ni zhi ba ste zhi ba de yang mi dmigs gang gi ni bde yang mi dmigs so//
212b3(mdo sde): 'jam dpal sngon byung ba 'das pa'i dus na/ bskal bzangs med/ bsam gyis mi khyab/ mtshungs pa med/ gzhal du med brjod du med pa'i pha rol gyi sang
212b4(mdo sde): ches pha rol na/ nyi ma snang ba zhes bya ba'i bskal pa la de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rig pa dang zhabs su ldan pa/ bde bar gshegs
212b5(mdo sde): pa/ 'jig rten mkhyen pa/ skyes bu 'dul ba'i kha lo sgyur ba/ bla na med pa/ lha dang mi rnams kyi ston pa sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das thams cad zil gyis gnon pa zhes bya ba 'a/
212b6(mdo sde): rten du byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad zil gyis gnon pa de'i rim gro byed pa'i dge slong zhi ba'i blo gros zhes bya ba zhig yod do// des de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis
212b7(mdo sde): gyis gnon pa la/ mo bye ba phrag brgyad cur bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub 'dod pa'i phyir yid du 'ong bas rim gro byas te/ yid du mi 'ong bas ma yin no// de bcom
213a1(mdo sde): rgan 'das de bzhin gshegs tha rnams cad zil gyis gnon padi'i kun du song nas 'di nad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das kyi sdus rgyas sa
213a2(mdo sde): 'tshal ba'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos chos gang la brtson par bgyi/ de skad ces gsol pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad zil gyis gnon pas dge
213a3(mdo sde): slong zhi ba'i blo gros la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// dge slong zhi ba'i blo gros sangs rgyas kyis la slob par 'dod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos/ sbyin
213a4(mdo sde): pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la brtson par bya'o// dge slong ji ltar spyad pas/ bdag sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur zhes byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' nan
213a5(mdo sde): pos/ sbyin pa'i ngo bo nyid mi dmigs par bya'i/ sbyin pa mi sbyin par ni mi bya'o// sbyin gnas kyi ngo bo nyid mi dmigs par bya'o/ sbyin gnas mi btsal bar ni mi bya'o//
213a6(mdo sde): bdag gi ngo bo nyid mi dmigs par bya'i sbyin bdag tu mi 'gyur bar ni mi bya'o// des las kyi rang bzhin mi dmigs par bya'i/ las bdag gir bya ba dang 'gal bar ni mi bya'o//
213a7(mdo sde): bslab la'i ngo bo nyid mi dmigs par bya'i/ sangs rgyas kyi ye shes la mi bslab par ni mi bya'o// sbyin pa de yang byang chub tu bsngo bar bya ste/ byang chub kyi ngom nyid dmigs par mi
213b1(mdo sde): bya bsngo ba'ija ba cad kyang dmigs par mibya/ dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams mi bsgo bar yang mi bya'o// dge slong 'di lnga snyed paran chu'i nAngan zla ba'i gzugs brnyan snang ba rnabs/
213b2(mdo sde): yang shes par mi bya/ de zla ba ma yin par shes par mi bya de bzhin du bya ba thams cad la yang shes par bya'o// bya ba de lta bus sbyin pa sbyin na sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin
213b3(mdo sde): yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ro// de nas dge slong zhi ba'i blo gros de la de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad zil gyis gnon pas sbyin pa de lta bus sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa
213b4(mdo sde): bstan pas sbyin pa yongs su bsngo ba'i ye shes dpag tu med pa dang ldan par gyur to// 'jam dpal de'i tshe de'i dus na gang bcom ldan 'das de bzhin
213b5(mdo sde): gshegs pa thams cad zil gyis gnon pa des/ sbyin pa bsngo ba'i snang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnyed par bya ba'i phyir btams pa dge slong zhi ba'i blo gros zhes bya bar gyur pa de

214a1(mdo sde): nub mngon par rdzogs pas sangs rgyas kyi bar du/ rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par byang chub sems dpa'i yon tan gzhan tshad med pa yongs su dag dang srung /

217a1(mdo sde): 'khor mo rin po che dang / glang po rin pon dang / rna rin po che dang / bud med rin po che dang / nor bu rin po che dang / khyim bdag rin po che dang rla

295a1(mdo sde): mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings dang / nam mkha' lta bur mi 'jig pa ste/ mya ngan las 'das pa'i sgra chos kyi dbyings kyi tshig gis 'das pa dang / byung ba dang //
295a2(mdo sde): 'byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis bsten te/ 'di ltar de bzhin gshegs pa rnams byung yang rung ma byung yang rung chos rnams kyi chos nyid chos kyi gnas
295a3(mdo sde): da dang / chos kyi dbyings dang / chos sbyor med pa nyid po 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa'o// rdo rje'i snying po skyon med pa zhes bya ba ni yang 'byung ba'i nyes pa thams cad dang bral ba'o//

295b1(mdo sde): rnam par shes pa'i yul rab tu rgyas pas sangs rgyas kyirgyas kyi rtso mched thams cad kyis kun nas miganas shing rdzogs par mi byed par 'gyur ba'i phyir mngon du ma thu nga

295b3(mdo sde): rnam pa sna tshogs kyi tshul gyi yul la nye bar spyod pa/ sprul pa'i yul can de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyis ting nge 'dzin las bslang ba'i sbyor bas brgyud pa las 'das pa chos kyi sprin

295b5(mdo sde): gyisar zhugs te thams cad du 'gro ba ma g.yos pa'i ting nge 'dzin spyod pa lhun gyis grub pa rtag pa/ zer zug pa/ brtan pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing stug po na gnas
295b6(mdo sde): bar 'gyur te/ rdo rje'i dbang po sa la dbang ba rnams la 'phrul pa'i 'jug pa ston par 'gyur te gnas gyur pa yid bzhin gyi ye shes dang / ting nge 'dzin can stobs dang
295b7(mdo sde): mngon par shes pa dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa dang / dbang la spyod pa ngang pa'i rgyal po dang 'dra bar ma zhugs pa'i chu'i zla ba lta bur 'gro ste/ blta ba'i don yod pa mi'i bdag po thams
296a1(mdo sde): cad kyi tshogs kyi 'khor du sems can rnams kyi bsam pa ji lta bur 'dod pa'i gzugs dag gis sangs rgyas kyi zhing stug po bstan pa'i phyir/ sems can gyisas/
296a2(mdo sde): pa bzhin du 'jug par 'gyur ro// 'dod pa'i khams kyi dbang po thams cad dang / dbang sgyur ba'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i nor bu rin po che'i snying po la sogs pa'i
296a3(mdo sde): gnas dag tu bde ba rnams myong bar byas te/ sa'i rim pa rnams bstan nas/ zhing nas zhing du phun sum bde ba rnams rab tu ston cing phyi ma'i mthar thug par sku grub
296a4(mdo sde): pa'i sngags 'chang ltar mi snang zhing / khang khyim gyi lha ltar de na gnas bzhin du mi snang ba'i gzugs su khyim na 'dug pa ltarade dag sprul pa'i 'od zer dang / 'phrul
296a5(mdo sde): pas sprul pa la spyod cing 'gro'o// song nas kyang de bzhir gshegs pa'i sprul pa'i sku nub ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku la zhen nas gnas par 'gyur ro// de nas bcom/
296a6(mdo sde): ldan 'das kyis tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gsungs so// dbang po phung po sprul yin te// srid dang ma rig las kyang min// bag chags kyis bcings mi bzad pa// yul dang dbang
296a7(mdo sde): po'i rgyu las byung // rnam pyod tshogs ni 'dod chags rnams// zhags pa sems spyod de yin no// khro ba ma lce mnyam pa ste// zhe sdang drug gi dngos po yin// thub spyod rnal 'byor/
296b1(mdo sde): bzang can gyi// 'di dag rtag tu rnam gzhigs te// phung po rnams ni dor ba'i phyir// rnal 'byor can gyis rnal 'byor spyod// gzugs ni 'byung ba'i tshogs yin te/
296b2(mdo sde): phung po'i lhag ma gzugs med la// ji bzhin par snang ri mo dang // grib ma stong du ma la sogs med// mkha'o la rlung gzugs mi snang dang // bya yi rjes rnams ji bzhin
296b3(mdo sde): ni/ mkhas pas so so rang rig pa// yang dag nyid dang yang dag mtha'// tshig gi spyod yul 'das pa ni// sangs rgyas dngos po mi snang ste// sangs rgyas sbas ni mya ngan 'das//
296b4(mdo sde): mya ngan 'das kyang sangs rgyas te// rnam rtog rtog dang bral bas na// de ni bstan du mi nus pa'i// rgyu dang 'bras bu med pa ste// yod dang med kyis rnam par spangs// rdo ba phye mar btag
296b5(mdo sde): pa la// gser ni yod par mi snang ste// sbyangs pa'i las kyi khyad par gyis// gser ni snang bar 'gyur ba yin// gzugs rnams rdul du rnam gzhigs te// mkhas pas phung po lhag
296b6(mdo sde): ma dang // khams dang skye mched tshogs rnams dang // rnam par shes dang dbang po dag/ gcig dang tha dad dngos por yang // rdul phran rnam par rab sbyangs na// dngos por sangs rgyas yod
296b7(mdo sde): pa mir// sangs rgyas med pa'ang ma yin te// rnal 'byor can rnams sangs rgyas mthong // mtshan rab sum cu rtsa gnyis can// gang na sdug bsngal de na bde// de nyid la ni snang ba yin/
297a1(mdo sde): sangs rgyas med ces mi bya ste// sangs rgyas mnyam par gzhag pa yod// rgyu yi sangs rgyas dge ba can// rtsa ba mkhas pa nyid kyang ste// 'jig rten kun gyi rgyal ba
297a2(mdo sde): dang / yang dag rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas dang // 'di dag sangs rgyas lngar gsungs so// sprul pa'i rgyal ba lhag ma rnams// de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po yid// mtshar rab sum cu rtsa gnyis
297a3(mdo sde): can// de bas sangs rgyas yod pa ste// rnal 'byor can gyis thub pa mthong // khams rnams gsum po 'das pa dang // rnam pa du mar sangs rgyas zhing // de bzhin gshegs kyi
297a4(mdo sde): lha rdzas zhing // rgyal sras bzang pos kun tu gang // de na thub chen sangs rgyas bzhugs// mtshan gyis kun nas yongs su rgyas// rnal 'byor rnal la mnyam par gzhag/ chos
297a5(mdo sde): dang bcas su rnam par mdzes// de bzhin phan tshun bsam gtan mdzad// shes rab ma shes shes byed la// stug po de na rnam par spyod// stug po de yi sems can su// sangs rgyas
297a6(mdo sde): gzugs can de dag kun// skad cig 'jig pa shin tu 'das// ting nge 'dzin la rtag tu mos// dka' ldan nas babs 'phrul pa gang // rtog pa can rnams kun gyis mthong // stug/
297a7(mdo sde): po nas gshegs glang po ste// sangs rgyas gzugs ni stug na bzhugs// sna tshogs rnam mang gzugs tshul te// sems can bsam bzhin zhugs pa'i sa// de bzhin gshegs pa mnyam
297b1(mdo sde): gzhag pa// chu yi zla ba bzhin du snang // sna tshogs gzug kyi nor bu ni// tshon gyi 'byor las rnam par mdzes// de bzhin sangs rgyas stug zhing na// mnyam par bzhag pas rnam
297b2(mdo sde): par mdzes// thams cad chos la gzugs brnyan ltar// gcig dang tha dad spangs pa ste// dgos par kun la 'jug pa ni// skyes bu dam pa thams cad mkhyen// rdul las ma yin dus las
297b3(mdo sde): min// dbang po las min gces las min// rkyen gyis ma yin 'jig rten dang // sangs rgyas ldan par rnam mdzes pa// rgyu yi tshul du sangs rgyas ni// 'bras bu rnams la rnam par mdzes//
297b4(mdo sde): 'jig rten sbrul 'khod bya ste// rgya mtsho ri dang shing dag dang // de la 'gro ba sna tshogs bcas// mnyam par bzhag pas shin tu dgyes// bya ba thams cad kyi nang du// gza' zla la sog
297b5(mdo sde): mdzes pa'i rnams// phyir yang phyag gis mthil bkod do// yungs 'brur 'gro ba kun 'dzud pa// sangs rgyas thub pa'i rnal 'byor mnga'// thub chen thub pa'i dam pa'o// 'jig
297b6(mdo sde): rten rnams la byed pa med// sangs rgyas 'phrul gyis sprul pa ste// 'byung ba gsum po 'di dag kun// sangs rgyas 'od kyis rnam par sprul// rab rib mi shes myos mdongs pa'i
297b7(mdo sde): rtog pa can rnams 'phyan pa yin// bdag dang bdag med lta ba'i rnams// yod dang med pa'i smra bas bcom// 'on tam thams cad 'jig pa dang // cung zad 'jig pas sla ba rnams// /
298a1(mdo sde): 'di la med dam cung zad dam// bdag dang bdag me dag la yod// sangs rgyas sna tshogs 'byung kun na// rnal 'byor mkhan po rnam par mdzes// dri za'i grog/
298a2(mdo sde): la bya ba rnams// ji ltar snang ba 'jig rten na// rmi lam rnam pa sna tshogs gzugs/ ri dgas rnams la smig rgyu bzhin// de bzhin 'jig rten sna tshogs dag gde ga la sogs
298a3(mdo sde): pa'i las rnams kyang // rlung ldan sogs pa'i thag pa bzhin// sangs rgyas rnal 'byor mkhyen pa'i mchog/ mo la 'khrul 'khor bskor ba ste// rgya mtsho skyab 'dzin dang 'dra// sdug
298a4(mdo sde): po'i ris kyi ye shes kyi rgyan las byung zhes bya ba'i le'u ste dang po'o// // de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa stan las langs te/ bla gos phrag pa gcig

298a6(mdo sde): su thal mo sbyar te phyag 'tshal nas bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das mtshams med pa lnga bgyid pa rnams dang / dam pa'i chos spong ba rnams dang /
298a7(mdo sde): 'phags pa spong ba rnams dang / mnar med pa la gzhol ba rnams dang / ma dang pha la snying ring ba rnams dang / tshangs pa 'gums pa rnams dang / la lang 'gums pa 'gungs pa'i sems can rnams
298b1(mdo sde): ji ltar yongs su 'grol bar 'gyur/ bcom ldan 'das sems can de dag 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal las ji ltar yongs su 'grol bar 'gyur/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/
298b2(mdo sde): 'jam dpal sbyin pa gnyis byin pa'i sems can rnams 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal las yongs su 'grol bar 'gyur te/ de 'di ltar chos kyi sbyin pa dang rang ming gi sbyin pa'o// sa
298b3(mdo sde): kyi sbyin pas skye ba dran par 'gyur ro// zang zing gi sbyin pas ni sems can thams cad la phan btags par 'gyur ro// zang zing gi sbyin pas ni bkris pa dang skom pa'i sdug bsngal yongs
298b4(mdo sde): su sbyong ngo // chos kyi sbyin pas ni sems can dmyale ba dang / grol song gi skye gnas dang gshin rje'i 'jig rten gyi 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal las yongs su 'grol to// 'jam
298b5(mdo sde): dpal sbyin pa gnyis po 'di byin na/ sbyin pa thams cad 'dus par 'gyur ro// 'jam dpal gzhan yang sbyin pa lngas sbyin pa dang / nye ba'i sbyin pa thams cad 'dus par 'gyur te/

299b1(mdo sde): ltung bag tshad brgya stong du mar skyes pa yod de/ yi dgas de bdag gi las kyi sdug bsngal mi bzad pa'i tshor ba yod do// 'jam dpal de bzhin du sems can sum do sde chen po rin po che 'di slong ba/

299b3(mdo sde): byug pa dang / phye ma dang / chos gos dang / gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / lha'i ba dan gyis mchod pa dang / chos smra ba de'ang mchod par bya ste/ ci ste myos smra ba de mtshams med

299b5(mdo sde): 'dug pa'i sha zos kyang / de dag thams cad phyir mi ldog par 'gyur te/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyang 'thob par 'gyur ro// ri dgas dang bya gzhan po de dag thams

300a1(mdo sde): par 'gyur ro// zos nas kyang mchod pa chen pos mchod par 'gyur ro// mdo rje thams cad 'dus pa'i rgyan stug po rin po che las sbyin pa'i le'u ste gnyis pa'o//

301a1(mdo sde): rnams kyi sgyu ma la// ji ltar gzhan du mthong ba dang // rmi lam na yang gzhan du ba'i// rmi lam bzhin du byis pas mthong // khyad par rab tu mthong ba ni// /

301a7(mdo sde): 'gyur ba chos tsam mo// kun tu phra ba'i bdag nyid kyi// yon tan dag tu dngos yod brtags// mar me bzhin du gsal byed pa// rgyu rnams dgos pa sgrub pa dag/ mtshan nyid snga nas mi
301b1(mdo sde): rnyed de// 'jig dang bral bas mi gnas pa'o// 'das pa 'das pa'i dngos por yang // yod pa ma yin 'byung ba med// rkyen du bla rnams med par yang // brtag pa'i dngos po klung
301b2(mdo sde): yang med// rkyeran rnams 'dus te byas pa la// dngos po yod pa ma yin te// rkyen rnams gang gi rkyen du 'gyur// yod dang med pa'i dngos mi snang // med pa'ang snang ba yod ma yin//
301b3(mdo sde): phra ba'i bdag gis rnam par brtags// phung po rdza ma ras la sogs// ri dgas skom gdungs smig rgyu bzhin// rmi lam dri za 'dra ba ste// btsug lag nor bu dug dang bcas// rab tu smra ba
301b4(mdo sde): sum brgya yis// 'jug pa dag dang phyir ldog dag/ mya ngan 'da' ba gang yang med/ de nas sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad rnam par bkod pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin ston
301b5(mdo sde): pa/ sa'i dbang po lag pa'i 'greng ba tshad med/ lus dpe med pa/ dpung rgyan dang / cod pan dang / gtsug gi rin po che dang / se mo dos shin tu chas pa stan las

303a1(mdo sde): 'das pa ste// sna tshogs gzugs kyi rin chen bzhin// de bzhin sangs rgyas sa bsam med// stug cing rgyal ba'i gnas gyur pa// ji ltar gyo mo rnams kyi rgyu/

303b1(mdo sde): rig pa'i ma bzhin du// bdag nyid zhir 'gyur de nyid du// de bzhin ltabs rnam brtags te// bdag med pasam gtan rab gnas pa// lba ba'i chos la bder gnas kyi// so so rang rig smra//

309a3(mdo sde): gsungs// phyi rol mtshan ma sems rnams dang // bag chags yid kyang de bzhin te// sems dang lhan cig ldan pa ni// khang pa la ni gnas pa yin// yid dang dbang por ldan pa ni// rnam shes/
309a4(mdo sde): lnga yi rgyu yin te// rtag tu yang dag ye shes kyis// 'jig rten rgyu la rnam par lta// de ltar byed dang bya ba med// de bzhin nyid 'di rnam gzhan min// thams cad chos kyi de bzhin nyid//
309a5(mdo sde): phan tshun stobs kyis 'byung ba ste// rnal 'byor can rnams de ltar lta// de bzhin nyid du gsal bar mthong // rang bzhin yongs su grub pa ni// chos rnams chos nyid de yin te// brtags pa'i
309a6(mdo sde): dngos po rang bzhin du// chos rnams thams cad ma skyes pa// stong pa ngo bo nyid med de// yod dang med pa'i phyogs spangs pa// sgyu ma rmi lam rnams dang 'dra// dri za'i grong khyer lta bu ste//
309a7(mdo sde): sna tshogs rnams dang smig rgya bzhin// du ba sprin stug lta bu ni// mtshan ma tshul dang dbyibs rnams kyis// ji ltar ming du 'jug pa yi// tshig dang yi ge mang po dang // ming rnams
309b1(mdo sde): mang po la yang ste// kun tu brtags pa'i rang bzhin yin// gzhan gyi dbang ni de las gzhan// yid don dbang po 'dus pa las// sa bon kun nas bag chags dang // tha dad ma yin
309b2(mdo sde): sems dang bcas// rnam par shes pa kun tu 'byung // gzhan gyi dbang gi rang bzhin yang // phan tshun stobs kyi rgyu las so// so so rang rig shin tu phra// mthong ba'i chos la gnas
309b3(mdo sde): pa ste// rang bzhin yongs su rdzogs pa 'di// 'phags pa rnams kyi spyod yul lo// 'phags pa'i rang bzhin thugs chud pas// sangs rgyas rnams dang sangs rgyas sras// rang

309b5(mdo sde): phyir chad 'byung ba med do zhes// sdug bsngal kun las rnam par grol// g.yo ba thams cad shin tu 'byung // bag chags ma lus bsregs pas na// rnam par rtog pa mi 'byung zhing // /
309b6(mdo sde): bdag med shin tu mthong ba ni// chos dang gang zag bsgrags pa ste// sa bon rnams dang phral bas na// sems kyi tshogs rnams mi 'jug go// thog ma med pa'i dus bsags pa'i//
309b7(mdo sde): yid kyi gnas ngan len rtog pa'i// spros pa thams cad mngon bsal bas// mya ngan 'das pa lcags bsregs bzhin// ji ltar rab tu bsregs pa'i lcags// bsil bar gyur kyang
310a1(mdo sde): 'jig pa med// de bzhin grol ba thams cad kyang // ma zad bzhin du bsil ba yi// zad pa med pa'i chos dbyings su// bzhugs pa stug po'i dkyil 'khor na/
310a2(mdo sde): rgyal ba rnams dang rgyal sras bcas// ting nge 'dzin gyi zas gnas pas// mnyam par gzhag la mnyam gzhag cing // mthong ba'i chos la bde bar gnas// rgyal po rnal 'byor can gyi
310a3(mdo sde): yul/ rnal 'byor 'di yin brnam par gyis// de ste rgyal sras dge ba'i gnas// stug por 'gro bar 'dod na ste// sangs rgyas thams cad bzhugs pa'i gnas// zhing gi mchog

310a5(mdo sde): rnam rtog 'byung // grub pa rnams ni ma gtogs par// rdza la sogs pa dbang po'i yul// phung po yon tan ldan pa'i rnams// rnam par rtog pa'i mtshan ma 'di// skye ba la

316a3(mdo sde): tshogs lta bu'am// byed dang las kyis ma byas shing // dbang po ku be ras ma byas// mchod sbyin sbyin sreg mchod 'bras sam// smyung gi gzhung gi lam gyis sam/ rlu rnams
316a4(mdo sde): shin tu phal che bas// nan tan rtag pa ma yin te// 'gro ba 'dzin pa med pa'ang min// rgyu rnams kyi yang rgyu dag ste// 'gro ba ngo bo nyid kyis grub// las kyi bag chags rnams las

316a7(mdo sde): mtshan// nyi zla gnyis kyi 'od zer bzhin// de ltar skyes bu gnas pa yin// dgos dang byed pa med pa ste// yod dang med kyi phyogs kyis spangs// gcig dang tha dad med pa/
316b1(mdo sde): ste/ mur 'dug phyogs kyis rnam par spangs// rjes su 'gro ba'i shes pa med// nam yang rnam par mi rtag ste// grol ba'i so so rang rig pa// sangs rgyas sar skyes rbab/

316b6(mdo sde): bzhin/ las kyi rlung gis skor byed pa// ji ltar rdza mkhan 'khor lo dang // lag dang thal zhar bskor ba yis// kun tu bskur cing snod byed pa// yon tan sna tshogs rnam par ldan/

317a1(mdo sde): mkha'i skar tshogs ji bzhin du// gnas shing rnam pa sna tshogs rnams// rlung gi rta sris shin tu bskor// ji ltar mkha' la bya rnams kyi// rjes ni snang ba
317a2(mdo sde): ma yin te// bar snang yod pa ma yin na'ang // bya rnams rgyu ba'i byed pa med// de bzhin rnam par shes pa'i mi// bdag yod ma yin gzhan med min// rnam dag par snang 'dra ba

317a4(mdo sde): zla ba yod pa ste// pad+mo'i 'dab ma de bzhin du// mig la bud med gzhon nu dag/ mig gis mthong bar cir mi 'gyur// de bzhin kun ga zhes par shes// las rnams cig car
317a5(mdo sde): byed pa ste// 'gro bdag gi lus la ni// khyab gnas sa bon can kun no// stug po'i sprin dang 'dra bar yang // sa rnams yog par shin tu gnas// tshe dang rnam shes

362b2(mdo sde): ldan pa yi// lus can rnams kyis rtag tu 'thob// de phyir rgyal ba'i sras rnams kyis// theg pa che la brtsod par gyis// mthar gyis bde gshegs gnas rab dang // rgyal po rtag tu'ang 'gyur bar 'ong // kun nas
362b3(mdo sde): nyon mongs chos rnams dang // rnam par byang ba'i yod pa kun// rtag tu lus can thams cad kyi// sa la kun gzhi 'byung ba yin// spyi dang rgyu rnams lhan cig gam// 'on tam spyi dang dbang pos kyang // gtso bo rkyen dang
362b4(mdo sde): rgyu rnams kyi// 'jig rten rab tu bsgrub par byas// khyad par can gyi rgyu brjod pa// ci nas 'byung bar 'gyur ba ste// rgyu med par yang med par 'gyur// bya med pa yang med par 'gyur// rnam par byang dang tha bi dang /
362b5(mdo sde): kun gzhi tha dad 'gyur ba min// de snyed rnam byang tha dad na// kun gzhi rtag pa ma yin 'gyur// sngon med 'jigs med rtag pa ste// mtha' bzhi rnam par spangs pa yin// de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po dag
362b6(mdo sde): sprul pa ye shes sgrar yang grags// phan tshun snying po tha mi dad// da ni sor gdub bzhin du gnas// sa rnams sna tshogs kun gzhi ste// bde gshegs snying po dge ba'ang de// snying po de la kun gzhi sgras// de bzhin
362b7(mdo sde): gshegs pa ston pa mdzad// snying po kun gzhir bsgrags par yang // blo nad rnams kyis mi shes so// gser mgar mkhas pas rnam dag gis// gser las sor gdub byas pa ni// sor mo rnams la rnam par mdzes// phan tshun tha dad
363a1(mdo sde): mtshan yin te// sor gdub ces kyang brjod mod kyi// las kyi mkhan pos yongs bsgyur bas// gser ni gzugs bzhin rab tu gnas// chos mthong rnal 'byor ldan pa yi// sems dang rnam par shes pa'i/
363a2(mdo sde): yul// bdun pa'i sa ni rnyed pa dang // 'byung ba las kyang rnam par ldog/ 'phags pa mthong ba'i chos ldan gyi// so so rang rig mthong ba dang // spyi dang bdag gi legs 'phags pa// thams cad brjod par mi nus so// ji snyed
363a3(mdo sde): yul yod ci yang rung // sems dang rnam shes spyod yul du// sna tshogs snang ba de dag kyang // rnam shes yin te yul med do// sems ni rnam pa gnyis dngos su// gzung dang 'dzin par snang ba ste// rdza phru snam bu sogs pa
363a4(mdo sde): yi yul ni gang yang yod pa min// ji ltar ri rab brten byas shing // nyi zla gza' yi tshogs kyi rnams// bral ba med par rtag 'brang ngo // de bzhin rnam dag kun gzhi la// rnam dag 'phags pa'i spyod yul ni// rtag par gser
363a5(mdo sde): bzhin rab tu 'bar// kun gzhi snying por bsgrags pa ni// rtog pa'i sems kyi yul ma yin// rang bzhin rnam par brtags pa dang // rtogs par nus pa ma yin dang // yongs su grub pa'i rang bzhin
363a6(mdo sde): yang / rnal 'byor thub can rtag tu mthong // yid kyi rnam shes yul can ni// bus pa rnams la 'ching ba'i dngos// sdig rgyas tshogs byung ba ste// 'phags pa rnams kyis ji med gzigs/
363a7(mdo sde): stong phrag bcu gnyis pa'i rgyan chug po las/ ji lta brjod pa'i mdo rdzogs so// / bsgyur ba ma rdzogs par bshes rgyam sa
363b1(mdo sde): A n+yatsa tu ras t+ya su tra khor spang du/ 'phags pa bden pa 'azhi'i mdo// sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skar bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das dmar bungan/
363b2(mdo sde): gyi grong khyer dang rgyal po'i khab kyi bar gyi dbus na/ rgyal po'i ma'i dbyug pa can nub mo nye bar rten cing / dge slong gi dge 'dun chen po dang thabs cig tu bzhugs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis/
363b3(mdo sde): dge slong rnams la bka' stsal pa dge slong dgang dang khyed cag kho nas 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi po de dag ma shes/ ma mthong khong du ma chung/ so sor ma rtogs pas lam ring po 'dir rgyu
363b4(mdo sde): cing 'khor bar gyur to// bzhi po de gang zhe na/ nga dang khyed cag kho nas sdug bsngal 'phags pa'i bden pa ma shes ma mthong / khong du ma chud/ so sor ma rtogs pas lam
363b5(mdo sde): ring po 'dir rgyug cing 'khor bar gyur to// nga dang khyed cag kho nas sdug bsngal kun 'byung 'phags pa'i bden pa ma shes/ ma mthong / khong du ma chud/ so sor ma rtogs pas lam ring po 'dir rgyug cing

363b7(mdo sde): kho nas sdug bsngal 'gog pa lam 'phags pa'i bden pa ma shes / ma mthong / khong du ma chud/ so sor ma rtogs pas lam ring po 'dir rgyug cing 'khor bar gyur to// dge slong dag ngas sdug bsngal 'phags pa
364a1(mdo sde): bder pa rjes su rtogs shing so sor rtogs te/ srid pa'i sred pa bcad pas 'khor ba'i skye ba zad de/ da ni srid pa gzhan med do// ngas sdug bsngal kur 'byung ba 'phags
364a2(mdo sde): pa'i bden pa rjes su rtogs shing so sor rtogs te/ srid pa'i sred pa de bcad pas 'khor ba'i skye ba zad de/ da ni srid pa gzhan med do// ngas sdug bsngal 'gog pa 'phags pa'i bden pa rjes su
364a3(mdo sde): rtogs shing so sor rtogs te/ srid pa'i sred pa de bcad pas 'khor ba'i skye ba zad de/ da ni srid pa gzhan med do// ngas sdug bsngal 'gog par 'gro ba'i lam 'phags pa'i bden pa rjes su rtogs
364a4(mdo sde): shing so sor rtogs te/ srid pa'i sred pa de bcad pas 'khor ba'i skye ba zad de/ da ni srid pa gzhan med do// bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal te/ bde bar gshegs pas de skad gsungs
364a5(mdo sde): nas ston pas gzhan yang 'di skad bka' stsal to// nga dang khyed cag kho na yis// 'phags pa'i bden pa bani po dag/ ji lta ba bzhin ma mthong bas// lam ring du ni 'khor bar 'gyur/ bden pa de dag
364a6(mdo sde): mthong nas ni// srid pa'i sred pa bcad nas su// 'khor ba'i skye ba zang bas na// da ni srid pa gnar med do// bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / dge slong de
364a7(mdo sde): ngag yi rangs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la mngon par bstod do// 'phags pa bden pa bzhi'i mdo rdzogs so//
